<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Other Events. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A subsidiary of American Tower Corporation<span style="font-weight:bold"> </span>(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) has entered into a <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-binding</span> term sheet contemplating a third party minority equity investment in the Company&#8217;s U.S. data center business in the anticipated amount of approximately $2.5&#160;billion. The valuation of the U.S. data center business in the investment is anticipated to be consistent with the valuation for the Company&#8217;s previously completed acquisition of CoreSite Realty Corporation and the valuations for the Company&#8217;s previously acquired data centers businesses. The term sheet is <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-binding,</span> and there are no assurances that the parties will enter into definitive agreements for, or complete, such investment or that any such investment would be on the terms described herein. </p>
